-- If you update the schema, in addition to updating this file, you should
-- find the version migration script in the config/incremental directory and
-- update that as well.  If it doesn't exist then you're the lucky person who
-- gets to create it!  It's name should be in the form of
-- r<new_version>-from-<old_version>.sql, i.e. r2.4.10-from-r2.4.9.sql

SET names utf8;

-- Table used to save adhoc queries for users
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS adhoc_queries;
CREATE TABLE adhoc_queries (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  user_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  name                  VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
  query                 TEXT NOT NULL,
  is_default            BOOL NOT NULL,
  description           TEXT NULL,

  last_executed         DATETIME NULL,
  execution_count       INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(user_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS adhoc_query_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE adhoc_query_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  adhoc_query_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(adhoc_query_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS approvers;
CREATE TABLE approvers (
  id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  approval_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  user_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  approved             ENUM ('In Progress', 'Need Info', 'Approved', 'Rejected', 'Canceled')
                       NOT NULL,
  canceled_reason      TEXT NULL,
  canceler_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  comments             TEXT NULL,
  date_approved        DATETIME NULL,
  reminder_active      BOOL NOT NULL default 1,
  fyi                  BOOL NOT NULL default 0,
  approver_role_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated              DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by           VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip        VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created              DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by           VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip        VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(approval_id),
  INDEX(user_id),
  INDEX (approver_role_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS shared_query_infos;
CREATE TABLE shared_query_infos (
  query_id              int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL default '0',
  user_id               int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL default '0',
  hide                  tinyint(1)       NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY           (query_id, user_id),
  INDEX                 (user_id, query_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
  id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL auto_increment,
  action                 ENUM('Add', 'Modify', 'Remove',
                              'Email', 'Cancel', 'Event') NOT NULL,
  field                  VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
  old_value              TEXT NULL,
  new_value              TEXT NULL,
  modified               TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  modified_by_user_id    INTEGER NOT NULL,
  modified_by            VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  modified_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  primary key (id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS biz_events;
CREATE TABLE biz_events (
  # Event fields
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  event_type          VARCHAR(32)   NOT NULL,
  event_owner_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  event_date          DATETIME     NOT NULL,
  title               VARCHAR(255)  NOT NULL,
  description         VARCHAR(255)  NULL,

  # Reminder fields
  days_notice         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  reminder_date_dnz   DATETIME     NOT NULL,
  notified_date       DATETIME     NULL,
  notify_to           VARCHAR(255)  NULL,
  notify_cc           VARCHAR(255)  NULL,

  # Auditable fields
  updated               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(event_owner_id),
  INDEX(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contacts;
CREATE TABLE contacts (
  id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  email_address   VARCHAR(80) NOT NULL,
  first_name      VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL,
  last_name       VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL,
  title           VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  address         VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  city            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  state           VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  zip             VARCHAR(20) NULL,
  country         VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  work_phone      VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  mobile_phone    VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  fax             VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  contact_type    ENUM('Business Contact',
                       'Tech Contact',
                       'Finance Contact',
                       'Legal Contact',
                       'Other',
                       'Business/Tech Contact') NOT NULL,
  notes           TEXT NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(email_address),
  INDEX(last_name)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contact_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE contact_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  contact_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(contact_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_terms;
CREATE TABLE contract_terms (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  section            VARCHAR(80) NOT NULL,
  language           TEXT NOT NULL,
  comments           TEXT NOT NULL,
  is_draft           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_fallback        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  fallback_status    ENUM('NA', 'NEEDS_REVIEW', 'REVIEWED',
                          'REQUIRES_APPROVAL', 'APPROVED'),
  updated            DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by         VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  updated_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  created            DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by         VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  created_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  deleted            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(section)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_term_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE contract_term_audit_logs (
  id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  contract_term_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(contract_term_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_term_categories;
CREATE TABLE contract_term_categories (
  contract_term_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  category_term_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(contract_term_id, category_term_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_term_category_service_types;
CREATE TABLE contract_term_category_service_types (
  reference_term_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_type_name VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS fallback_term_service_types;
CREATE TABLE fallback_term_service_types (
  fallback_term_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_type       VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(fallback_term_id, service_type)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS countries;
CREATE TABLE `countries` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `country_code` varchar(8) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(45) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `region_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `sub_region` varchar(120) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'N/A',
  `require_postal_code` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `governing_law_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `region_id` (`region_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=252 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_bodies;
CREATE TABLE deal_bodies (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                    VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  partner_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  deal_count_dnz          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  termination_deal_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  needs_rebuilding        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  # Effectivity fields
  needs_effectivity_recalculation BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  effectivity_status_dnz  ENUM('UNINITIALIZED', 'SCUTTLED', 'PRE_SALES',
                               'PENDING', 'ACTIVE', 'EXPIRED', 'TERMINATED',
                               'UNKNOWN')
                            NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNINITIALIZED',
  effective_date_dnz      DATE NULL,
  termination_date_dnz    DATE NULL,
  auto_renewal_option_dnz VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT "noRenew",
  ultimate_termination_date_dnz  DATE NULL,

  # Client Id fields
  paying_status_dnz       ENUM('UNINITIALIZED', 'PRE_SALES', 'PENDING',
                               'PAYING', 'PLACEHOLDER', 'EXPIRED', 'TERMINATED',
                               'NA', 'UNKNOWN')
                            NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNINITIALIZED',
  content_owner_not_needed BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  payment_required         BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  # Audit columns
  updated               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  created               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  INDEX(name),
  INDEX(needs_rebuilding),
  INDEX(needs_effectivity_recalculation),
  INDEX(effectivity_status_dnz),
  INDEX(effective_date_dnz),
  INDEX(termination_date_dnz),
  INDEX(ultimate_termination_date_dnz),
  INDEX(paying_status_dnz)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_body_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE deal_body_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_body_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_body_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deals;
CREATE TABLE deals (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                    VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  legal_name_of_contracting_entity VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  use_as_reference        VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  non_std_lang_referral   TEXT NULL,
  partner_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  final_sales_approver_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  fin_manager_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_reviewer_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  sales_approver_id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_modeler_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_type               ENUM('Amendment', 'Extension','New','Renewal','Termination','Upsell') NOT NULL,
  parent_deal_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_body_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  contract_term           INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  typical_users           TEXT NULL,
  exclusivity             TEXT NULL,
  global_deal             TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0,
  -- TODO:  Get list of sales groups
  deal_revenue            DOUBLE NULL,
  rev_share               INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  currency_code           CHAR(3) NOT NULL,
  report_comments         TEXT NULL,
  notes                   TEXT NULL,
  approved_by_emg         ENUM('Not Required', 'Yes', 'No')
                          DEFAULT 'Not Required',
  emg_notes               TEXT NULL,
  countries_sorting_index TEXT NULL,
  deal_matter_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  pre_sales_status        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL default 0,
  reason_scuttled         TEXT NULL,
  post_sales_status       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL default 0,
  sign_date               DATE NULL,
  date_moved_to_100_percent_pre_sales_status DATE NULL,
  target_sign_date        DATE NULL,
  actual_launch_date      DATE NULL,
  expiration_date         DATE NULL,
  placeholder_extension_end_date DATE NULL,
  deal_folder_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  credit_check_requester_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  credit_check_requested_date DATETIME NULL,
  credit_check_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  credit_check_request_notes TEXT NULL,
  credit_check_request_amount DOUBLE NULL,
  rpm_estimate_id         INTEGER NULL,
  deal_model_requester_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_model_requested_date DATETIME NULL,
  deal_model_request_notes TEXT NULL,
  tech_profile_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  tech_approval_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  group_id                INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_model_required     BOOL NULL,
  strategic_value         ENUM('1', '2', '3', '4', '5') NULL,
  deal_tier               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  -- Payment Information
  payment_required       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  spm_required           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  payment_information_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,

  deal_risk               ENUM('highRisk', 'lowRisk') NULL,
  signatory_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  ask_for_parent_deal     BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  is_standard_deal        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  counter_signature_required BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  partner_acceptance_online BOOL NULL,
  partner_acceptance_method ENUM('MOCA',
                                 'MOCA_PLUS_ESIGN',
                                 'MOCA_PLUS_OFFLINE',
                                 'STANDARD_OFFLINE',
                                 'NON_STANDARD_OFFLINE',
                                 'NON_STANDARD_ONLINE'),
  client_ids_not_needed   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  -- Effectivity fields
  needs_effectivity_recalculation BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  effectivity_status_dnz  ENUM('UNINITIALIZED', 'SCUTTLED', 'PRE_SALES',
                               'PENDING', 'ACTIVE', 'EXPIRED', 'TERMINATED',
                               'UNKNOWN')
                            NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNINITIALIZED',
  effective_date_dnz      DATE NULL,
  termination_date_dnz    DATE NULL,
  is_termination_date_dnz_inherited  BOOL NULL DEFAULT 0,
  auto_renewal_option_dnz VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT "noRenew",
  ultimate_termination_date_dnz  DATE NULL,

  route_contract_to       ENUM('NA_CONTRACT_ADMIN',
                               'EMEA_CONTRACT_ADMIN',
                               'CHINA_CONTRACT_ADMIN',
                               'COMPLIANCE_COORDINATOR',
                               'LEGAL_ASSISTANTS',
                               'DUBLIN_CONTRACT_ADMIN')
                          NULL,

  content_licensing_detail_required BOOL NULL,
  content_licensing_detail_status  ENUM('SPD_PENDING',
                                        'LTM_PENDING',
                                        'LTM_IN_PROGRESS',
                                        'COMPLETED',
                                        'AMENDMENT_IN_PROGRESS',
                                        'AMENDED',
                                        'AMENDMENT_PENDING_ON_ROOT_DEAL'),
  draft_executive_summary_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  spd_note                TEXT NULL,
  salesforce_opportunity_id VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  double_click_deal_type ENUM('APA',
                              'NO_APA',
                              'AAA',
                              'EXTNSN',
                              'APA_EXH',
                              'BETA',
                              'DT_SOW',
                              'LTD_UA',
                              'NTA',
                              'TERMN'),
  -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(parent_deal_id),
  INDEX(deal_body_id),
  INDEX(name),
  INDEX(partner_id),
  INDEX(final_sales_approver_id),
  INDEX(fin_manager_id),
  INDEX(deal_reviewer_id),
  INDEX(sales_approver_id),
  INDEX(group_id),
  INDEX(deal_modeler_id),
  INDEX(deal_matter_id),
  INDEX(pre_sales_status),
  INDEX(post_sales_status),
  INDEX(needs_effectivity_recalculation),
  INDEX(effectivity_status_dnz),
  INDEX(effective_date_dnz),
  INDEX(termination_date_dnz),
  INDEX(ultimate_termination_date_dnz),
  INDEX(credit_check_requester_id),
  INDEX(rpm_estimate_id),
  INDEX(deal_model_requester_id),
  INDEX(final_sales_approver_id),
  INDEX(fin_manager_id),
  INDEX(sales_approver_id),
  INDEX(deal_reviewer_id),
  INDEX(deal_modeler_id),
  INDEX(signatory_id),
  INDEX(draft_executive_summary_id),
  INDEX(payment_information_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS payment_information;
CREATE TABLE payment_information (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  var_pmt_components      ENUM('', 'Yes', 'No') NULL,
  standard_tax_clause     BOOL NULL,
  payee_site_name         VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  vendor_name             VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  oracle_vendor_num       VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  payment_method          ENUM('Check', 'Electronic', 'Wire') NULL,
  payment_notes           TEXT NULL,
  deal_body_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,

    -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_body_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# Create table to audit log info for payment information
#

CREATE TABLE payment_information_audit_logs (
  id                       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  payment_information_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(payment_information_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE deal_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_status_logs;
CREATE TABLE deal_status_logs (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  old_pre_sales_status        INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  new_pre_sales_status        INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  old_post_sales_status       INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  new_post_sales_status       INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  modified_date               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_countries;
CREATE TABLE deal_countries (
  country_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(country_id, deal_id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_regions;
CREATE TABLE deal_regions (
  region_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(region_id, deal_id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_spds;
CREATE TABLE deal_spds (
  spd_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(spd_id, deal_id),
  INDEX(deal_id, spd_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# TODO(alexwu): rename the table to team_members later,
# do not rename the table for now due to other teams are using it.
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS deal_team_members;
CREATE TABLE deal_team_members (
  id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id          INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  misc_matter_id   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  deal_body_id     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  partner_id       INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  user_id          INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  role_id          INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  team_type        ENUM('DEAL', 'MISC_MATTER', 'DEAL_BODY', 'PARTNER') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'DEAL',
  primary_member   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE (deal_id, misc_matter_id, deal_body_id, partner_id, user_id, role_id),
  INDEX (misc_matter_id),
  INDEX (user_id),
  INDEX (role_id),
  INDEX (deal_body_id),
  INDEX (partner_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS deal_tams;
CREATE VIEW deal_tams AS
SELECT tm.user_id AS tam_id, d.id AS deal_id
FROM deals d
  JOIN deal_bodies db ON d.deal_body_id = db.id
  JOIN deal_team_members tm ON (db.id = tm.deal_body_id AND tm.role_id = 3);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS misc_matter_countries;
CREATE TABLE misc_matter_countries (
  country_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  misc_matter_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(country_id, misc_matter_id),
  INDEX(misc_matter_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS payment_form_requests;
CREATE TABLE payment_form_requests (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_body_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  security_key          VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  requester_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  request_date          DATE NOT NULL,
  request_details       TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(security_key, request_date),
  INDEX (deal_body_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Responsible for keeping track of uploaded documents.  Maps the names
-- presented in the application to the actual filesystem paths.
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS documents;
CREATE TABLE documents (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  misc_matter_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_folder_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  document_name         VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, -- name shown in app
  document_path         VARCHAR(512) NOT NULL,
  upload_date           DATETIME NOT NULL,
  document_type_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  user_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL, -- user who uploaded,
  comments              TEXT NULL,
  thread                INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  version               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted               BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  migration_status      ENUM('LOCAL_UNKNOWN', 'LOCAL_MISSING', 'LOCAL_VALID',
                          'REMOTE_READY', 'REMOTE_VALID', 'BLOBSTORE_READY', 'BLOBSTORE_VALID')
                          NOT NULL DEFAULT 'LOCAL_UNKNOWN',
  backup_path           VARCHAR(512),
  echo_sign_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(user_id),
  INDEX(misc_matter_id),
  INDEX(deal_folder_id),
  INDEX(document_type_id),
  INDEX(user_id),
  INDEX(migration_status),
  INDEX(echo_sign_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS document_types;
CREATE TABLE document_types (
  id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  category  ENUM ('business', 'legal', 'financial', 'tech_opt',
                  'customer_info') NOT NULL,
  descr     VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  deleted   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS comments;
CREATE TABLE comments (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  partner_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  deal_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  subject               VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  trakken_number        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  time_spent            FLOAT(6,2) NULL DEFAULT 0.0,
  details               TEXT NULL,
  type                  ENUM('Other',
                             'General Support/Planning',
                             'Optimizations',
                             'Re-launch/Modification',
                             'New Partner Launch',
                             'New Site Launch',
                             'New Service Launch',
                             'Alerts/Troubleshooting',
                             'Technical Reviews/Testing',
                             'Development/Integration',
                             'Content Update') NOT NULL,
  phase                 VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted               BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS entity_partner_contacts;
CREATE TABLE entity_partner_contacts (
  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  partner_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  entity_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  entity_type ENUM('DEAL','MISC_MATTER','LEAD', 'DEAL_BODY') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'DEAL',
  contact_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(partner_id),
  INDEX(entity_id),
  INDEX(entity_type),
  INDEX(contact_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF exists groups;
CREATE TABLE groups (
  id                                INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                              VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  descr                             VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  deprecated                        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  region_id                         INT(10) UNSIGNED,
  service_group_id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  org_id                            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  approverSelectionNotes            TEXT NULL,
  requires_technical_profile        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  uses_workflow                     ENUM('NONE', 'DOUBLECLICK', 'DVIP', 'ENTERPRISE') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'NONE',
  uses_media_buys_workflow          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  request_se_assignment             BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  request_tam_assignment            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  notify_tpm_deal_in_pipeline       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  notify_on_auto_renewal            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  use_group_in_closed_email_subject BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  notify_deal_closed_email          VARCHAR(50),
  notify_termination_date_approaching BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  credit_check_uses_pogo            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  external_documents_location_url   VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  support_standard_deal             BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  counter_signature_required        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  requires_fully_executed_contract_in_simba BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  uses_critical_dates               BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  allow_online_contract_agreements  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  automate_online_executive_summary BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  oes_template_id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  skip_compliance_approver          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  enable_contract_admin_request_checks                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  disable_ca_request_for_non_std                       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  disable_tech_profile_deal_model_requests_forstd      BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  enable_deal_folder_creation_checks                   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  audit_deal_folder_email           BOOL DEFAULT 1,
  category                          VARCHAR(30),
  product_area_id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  is_sensitive                      BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  support_oti                       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated                           DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id                INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                        VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip                     VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                           DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id                INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                        VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip                     VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(name),
  INDEX(descr),
  INDEX(oes_template_id),
  INDEX(aas_template_id),
  INDEX(product_area_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS group_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE group_audit_logs (
  id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  group_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(group_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

                                         'Very basic system access');

-- Table for persisting SimbaLabel objects.
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS labels;
CREATE TABLE labels (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  owner_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  name                  VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  background_color      CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  foreground_color      CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted               BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  UNIQUE (owner_id, name),
  INDEX (id),
  INDEX (owner_id, name),
  INDEX (name)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Join table for labels and entities.
-- entity_id refers to the entity's primary key, such as deals.id.
-- This creates a bidirectional many-to-many mapping between labels and entities.
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS entity_labels;
CREATE TABLE entity_labels (
  label_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  entity_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  entity_type           ENUM('DEAL','PARTNER','MISC_MATTER','DEAL_BODY', 'LEAD') NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (entity_type, entity_id, label_id),
  INDEX (label_id),
  INDEX (entity_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS legal_groups;
CREATE TABLE legal_groups (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                  VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  descr                 TEXT NOT NULL,
  is_contract_admin_using_trakken BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  contract_admin_trakken_email_address VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  email_contract_admins_and_trakken BOOL NULL DEFAULT 0,
  enable_contract_admin BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_system_group       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_ops_group          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cta_country_legal_groups;
CREATE TABLE cta_country_legal_groups (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  country_name       VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  short_country_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  legal_group_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(country_name),
  UNIQUE INDEX(short_country_name)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cta_legal_form_mappings;
CREATE TABLE cta_legal_form_mappings (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  /* "LegalForm" name matches name on legal_ndas table */
  LegalForm             VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  agreement_type_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  agreement_sub_type_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  document_type_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(LegalForm)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tasks;
CREATE TABLE tasks (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  /* Core properties */
  task_type                   ENUM('CONTRACT_INTEGRITY_REVIEW', 'PERMISSION_REQUEST_MANAGER',
                              'LEGAL_REQUEST', 'CONTRACT_ADMIN_REQUEST', 'SYMPHONY_TASK', 'APPROVER_TASK'
                              ) NOT NULL,
  status                      ENUM('NEW', 'ASSIGNED', 'COMPLETED', 'CANCELED',
                              'APPROVED', 'REJECTED', 'NEED_INFO', 'INFORMED', 'NONE') NOT NULL,
  archived                    BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  description                 TEXT NULL,
  comments                    TEXT NULL,
  requester_id                INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,

  /* Assignment */
  assignee_id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  assigned_date               DATETIME NULL,

  /* Dates */
  target_completion_date      DATE NULL,
  actual_completion_date      DATETIME NULL,

  /* Audit Fields */
  updated                     DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by                  VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  updated_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  created                     DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by                  VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  created_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(status),
  INDEX(requester_id),
  INDEX(assignee_id),
  INDEX(task_type)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS task_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE task_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  task_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(task_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS task_attributes;
CREATE TABLE task_attributes (
  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  task_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  type ENUM('INTEGER', 'STRING', 'DATE', 'FLOAT', 'BOOLEAN', 'LIST', 'PROTO') NOT NULL,
  attribute_key VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL,
  attribute_value VARCHAR(256)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_integrity_review_tasks;
CREATE TABLE contract_integrity_review_tasks (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS legal_request_tasks;
CREATE TABLE legal_request_tasks (
  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  nda_status ENUM('YES', 'NO', 'UNKNOWN', 'NOT_NEEDED') DEFAULT 'UNKNOWN',
  PRIMARY KEY (id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS symphony_tasks;
CREATE TABLE symphony_tasks (
  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
  symphony_task_id VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL,
  execution_id VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL,
  task_executor_name VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL,
  event_type VARCHAR(256),
  dedup_token_time_ms BIGINT UNSIGNED,
  key_value_string TEXT,
  transfer_metadata_string TEXT
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS approver_tasks;
CREATE TABLE approver_tasks (
  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  approval_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  approver_role_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  approver_task_type enum('SPECIAL', 'DEAL_FOLDER'),
  reminder_active TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  PRIMARY KEY (id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS task_entities;
CREATE TABLE task_entities (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  task_id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  entity_type             ENUM('DEAL','MISC_MATTER','LEAD', 'DEAL_BODY', 'USER', 'PARTNER', 'GROUP', 'LEGAL_ENTITY',
                            'LEGAL_GROUP', 'DEAL_FOLDER', 'LEGAL_MATTER', 'DEAL_MATTER', 'DEAL_MISC_MATTER',
                            'SPECIAL_APPROVAL', 'RELATED_MATTER', 'STANDARD_NDA', 
                            'CONTRACT_TEMPLATE_VERSION', 'MANAGER_PERMISSION_REQUEST_TASK',
                            'DEAL_FOLDER_APPROVAL', 'DVIP_DEAL_DETAIL') NOT NULL,
  entity_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,

  -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(task_id),
  INDEX(entity_type),
  INDEX(entity_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS partners;
CREATE TABLE partners (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                  VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
  descr                 TEXT NULL,
  partner_service_tier  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  partner_category      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  notification          TEXT NULL,
  esc_procedures        TEXT NULL,
  sensitivities         TEXT NULL,
  filtering_blocking    TEXT NULL,
  special_impl_notes    TEXT NULL,
  trade_name            VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  billing_address       TEXT NULL,
  parent_account_name_term_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  primary_tam_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  ranking_score         DOUBLE NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;
  -- Effectivity fields
  needs_effectivity_recalculation BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  effectivity_status_dnz  ENUM('UNINITIALIZED', 'SCUTTLED', 'PRE_SALES',
                               'PENDING', 'ACTIVE', 'EXPIRED', 'UNKNOWN')
                            NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNINITIALIZED',
  address_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  imported_from         ENUM('MISC_MATTERS', 'STIPULATE') NULL,
  duplicate             BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  creation_reason       VARCHAR(512),
  num_of_clientids     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  num_of_techreviews   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  num_of_launches      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  num_of_optimizations INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  num_of_comments      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  latest_techreview    DATETIME NULL,
  latest_launch        DATE NULL,
  latest_optimization  DATETIME NULL,
  latest_comment       DATETIME NULL,
  fully_launched       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  needs_recalculation  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  oti                  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  co_advisors          VARCHAR(200) NULL,
  -- Audit fields
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  grm_id                INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  customer_master_id    VARCHAR(16) DEFAULT NULL,
  simple_name           VARCHAR(200) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(needs_effectivity_recalculation),
  INDEX(effectivity_status_dnz),
  INDEX(address_id),
  INDEX(needs_recalculation),
  INDEX(parent_id),
  INDEX(name)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS partner_links;

)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS partner_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE partner_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  partner_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(partner_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS regions;
CREATE TABLE regions (
  id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name  VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  parent_region_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  deleted  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS review_forum_infos;
CREATE TABLE review_forum_infos (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL auto_increment,
  deal_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  review_forum       ENUM('EMG', 'EMEA_FMG', 'SYN_FMG', 'PC_FMG', 'GMC', 'MEDIA_SOL',
                          'DISTR_COUNCIL', 'JAPAC_FMG', 'OC_DEAL',
                          'BC_DEAL', 'FMG_DEAL', 'DOTORGX', 'GBX', 'GMX', 'ENTX', 'EPX', 'HWX', 'PBX', 'PPX', 'YTX', 'GOOGLE_X', 'IMPACT_X', 'SAC', 'GHM', 'AEX') NOT NULL,
  meeting_date       DATETIME NULL,
  approval_status    ENUM('APPROVED', 'REJECTED', 'APPROVAL_NOT_REQUIRED') NOT NULL,
  request            TEXT NOT NULL,
  outcome            TEXT NULL,
  updated            DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created            DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS review_forum_info_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE review_forum_info_audit_logs (
  id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  review_forum_info_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(review_forum_info_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

drop table if exists roles;
CREATE TABLE roles (
  id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name            VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  display_name    VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  deleted         BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_system_role  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  popularity      INTEGER UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  sensitive_role  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  department      VARCHAR(30),
  description     VARCHAR(200),
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS service_types;
CREATE TABLE service_types (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                    VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  display_name            VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  uses_client_ids         BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  uses_content_licensing_details BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  uses_common_service     BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  is_media_buy_service    BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_sla_service          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  uses_content_owner_details   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  deleted                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  service_group_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  max_tier                INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  help_text               TEXT NULL,
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(name),
  INDEX(service_group_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS services;
CREATE TABLE services (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_type_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_type                VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNKNOWN',
  class_discriminator         VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'COMMON',
  launched                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_matter_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  notes                       TEXT NULL,
  tier                        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  sla_uptime                  ENUM('No SLA', '99.5', '99.9', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_uptime_custom           TEXT NULL,
  sla_server_latency          ENUM('No SLA', '800', '1200', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_server_latency_custom   TEXT NULL,
  sla_network_latency         ENUM('No SLA', '400', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_network_latency_custom  TEXT NULL,
  sla_grace_period            ENUM('No SLA', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_grace_period_custom     TEXT NULL,
  sla_allowed_scheduled_downtime ENUM('No SLA', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_allowed_scheduled_downtime_custom TEXT NULL,
  sla_severity_levels_and_response_time ENUM ('No SLA', 'Custom') NULL,
  sla_severity_levels_and_response_time_custom TEXT NULL,
  sla_service_incident_reporting ENUM('None', 'Monthly', 'Quarterly', 'Annually') NULL,
  sla_service_incident_reporting_custom TEXT NULL,
  sla_other                   TEXT NULL,
  post_sales_status           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated                     DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                     DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                     BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(service_type),
  INDEX(service_matter_id),
  INDEX(service_tier)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS service_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE service_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  service_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(service_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS service_matters;
CREATE TABLE service_matters (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL auto_increment,
  service_matter_type         ENUM('PS', 'AFC', 'AFS', 'AFD', 'AFE', 'WS', 'TB', 'GV')
                              NOT NULL,
  critical_dates_id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,

  -- Common columns to AFS, AFC, AFD, AFE
  branding_requirements                 TEXT NULL,
  downloadable_flag                     BOOL NULL,
  downloadable                          TEXT NULL,
  google_guarantees                     DOUBLE NULL,
  deduction                             INTEGER NULL,
  attribution_requirements              TEXT NULL,
  filtering_requirements_flag           BOOL NULL,
  filtering_requirements                TEXT NULL,
  customer_revenue_share                INTEGER NULL,
  google_revenue_share                  INTEGER NULL,
  service_level_agreement_flag          BOOL NULL,
  service_level_agreement               TEXT NULL,
  distribution_rights_flag              BOOL NULL,
  distribution_rights                   TEXT NULL,
  reporting_flag                        BOOL NULL,
  reporting                             TEXT NULL,
  notes                                 TEXT NULL,

  -- afc service matter
  domains                               TEXT NULL,

  -- afs service matter
  customer_guarantees                   DOUBLE NULL,

  -- afe and afd service matter
  google_hosted_flag                    BOOL NULL,
  google_hosted                         TEXT NULL,

  -- afe service matter
  custom_landing_page_flag              BOOL NULL,
  custom_landing_page                   TEXT NULL,

  -- Printer Service Matter
  branding_requirements_flag            BOOL NULL,
  initial_num_titles                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  total_titles_in_print                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  viewable_percentage                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  explicit_revenue_share                TEXT NULL,
  explicit_revenue_share_flag           BOOL NULL,
  explicit_excerpt_requirements         TEXT NULL,
  explicit_excerpt_requirements_flag    BOOL NULL,
  image_blocking                        TEXT NULL,
  image_blocking_flag                   BOOL NULL,
  geostrict_language                    TEXT NULL,
  geostrict_language_flag               BOOL NULL,
  ads                                   TEXT NULL,
  ads_flag                              BOOL NULL,
  additional_security_requirements      TEXT NULL,
  additional_security_requirements_flag BOOL NULL,
  syndication_rights_limited            TEXT NULL,
  syndication_rights_limited_flag       BOOL NULL,
  two_page_limit_flag                   BOOL NULL,
  two_page_limit                        TEXT NULL,
  obligation_to_make_inaccessible_flag  BOOL NULL,
  obligation_to_make_inaccessible       TEXT NULL,
  authorized_users_lang_flag            BOOL NULL,
  authorized_users_lang                 TEXT NULL,
  non_authorized_users_lang_flag        BOOL NULL,
  non_authorized_users_lang             TEXT NULL,
  ads_need_label_flag                   BOOL NULL,
  ads_need_label                        TEXT NULL,
  ads_need_removal_in_timeframe_flag    BOOL NULL,
  ads_need_removal_in_timeframe         TEXT NULL,
  ads_blocklist_flag                    BOOL NULL,
  ads_blocklist                         TEXT NULL,
  ads_ad_safe_flag                      BOOL NULL,
  ads_ad_safe                           TEXT NULL,
  buy_link_flag                         BOOL NULL,
  buy_link                              TEXT NULL,
  ggl_must_remove_results_flag          BOOL NULL,
  ggl_must_remove_results               TEXT NULL,
  ggl_must_delete_content_flag          BOOL NULL,
  ggl_must_delete_content               TEXT NULL,
  ggl_must_remove_results_upon_term_flag   BOOL NULL,
  ggl_must_remove_results_upon_term        TEXT NULL,
  ggl_must_delete_content_upon_term_flag   BOOL NULL,
  ggl_must_delete_content_upon_term        TEXT NULL,
  content_modifying_restrictions_flag      BOOL NULL,
  content_modifying_restrictions           TEXT NULL,
  ggl_must_destroy_books_flag              BOOL NULL,
  ggl_must_destroy_books                   TEXT NULL,
  redist_restrictions_flag                 BOOL NULL,
  redist_restrictions                      TEXT NULL,
  auto_renew_language_deleted_flag         BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  auto_renew_language_deleted              TEXT NULL,
  new_gp_request                           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  -- websearch service matter
  marketing_flag                        BOOL NULL,
  marketing                             TEXT NULL,
  websearch_pricing                     DOUBLE NULL,

  -- toolbar

  dist_apps_bundled_with_ggl_flag   BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  dist_apps_bundled_with_ggl        TEXT NULL,
  third_party_in_bundle_flag        BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  third_party_in_bundle             TEXT NULL,
  third_party_dist_flag             BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  third_party_dist                  TEXT NULL,
  exclusivity_flag                  BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  exclusivity                       TEXT NULL,
  min_dist_commitment_flag          BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  min_dist_commitment               TEXT NULL,
  max_dist_commitment_flag          BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  max_dist_commitment               TEXT NULL,
  ggl_guaranteed_min_payment_flag   BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  ggl_guaranteed_min_payment        TEXT NULL,
  sell_off_period                   INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  ggl_reporting_oblig_flag          BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  ggl_reporting_oblig               TEXT NULL,
  liability_cap                     TEXT NULL,
  ggl_term_rights_flag              BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  ggl_term_rights                   TEXT NULL,
  dist_term_rights_flag             BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  dist_term_rights                  TEXT NULL,

  -- google video
  agreement_type                               VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  content_license_grant                        VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  content_license_grant_explanation            TEXT NULL,
  provider_brand_features_license              VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  provider_brand_features_license_explanation  TEXT NULL,
  termination                                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  termination_explanation                      TEXT NULL,
  indemnity                                    VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  other_special_terms                          TEXT NULL,

  -- general auditing
  updated                               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip                         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip                         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                               BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(service_matter_type)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS special_approvals;
CREATE TABLE special_approvals (
  id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  approval_type   enum('SPECIAL_APPROVAL',
                       'FINANCE_APPROVAL',
                       'SALES_APPROVAL',
                       'MEDIA_BUY_EXTENSION_APPROVAL',
                       'MISC_MATTER_APPROVAL',
                       'MOCA_APPROVAL',
                       'DVIP_WORKFLOW_APPROVAL'
                       ) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'SPECIAL_APPROVAL',
  fsa             BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  tentative       TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0,
  deal_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  misc_matter_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
-- User who made the approval request.  Approvers are stored in their own
-- table since there can be more than one.
  user_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  subject               VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
  request               TEXT NOT NULL,
  date_requested        DATETIME NOT NULL,
  date_required         DATE,
  canceled              BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  canceled_reason       TEXT NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(misc_matter_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# Create table for moca special approval to sub class special_approvals
#

  id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  instruction TEXT,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
  )ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS special_approval_audit_logs;

  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  approval_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(approval_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS special_approval_documents;
CREATE TABLE special_approval_documents (
  approval_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  document_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(approval_id, document_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users;
CREATE TABLE users (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  user_type               ENUM('REGULAR', 'USER_GROUP') NOT NULL,
  username                VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  descr                   TEXT NULL,
  email                   VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  first_name              VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  last_name               VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  has_doppleganger        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

-- title_role_id references a single role that contains the user's official
-- job title.  This is largely used for display purposes (many job titles
-- have SE privileges, but an SPD doesn't want to see "Sales Engineer" next
-- to their name.  The user_roles table is used for the actual authorization
-- logic.
  title_role_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  is_beta_tester          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_system_user          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  enabled                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  muted_notification_type TEXT NULL,
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  ooo_flag                BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ooo_start_date          DATETIME NULL,
  ooo_end_date            DATETIME NULL,
  ooo_instructions        TEXT NULL,
  delegatee_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  delegation_status       ENUM('NA', 'NOT_STARTED', 'STARTED', 'COMPLETED') DEFAULT 'NA',
  last_announcement_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  preferences_json        TEXT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(username),
  INDEX(first_name),
  INDEX(last_name),
  INDEX(title_role_id),
  INDEX(delegatee_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO users
 (user_type, username, descr,
  email, first_name, last_name,
  title_role_id, is_beta_tester, is_system_user, enabled,
  updated, updated_by_user_id, updated_by, updated_by_ip,
  created, created_by_user_id, created_by, created_by_ip)
VALUES
 ('REGULAR', 'simbasystem', 'Simba System User',
  'simba-system@google.com', 'Simba', 'System',
  65, 0, 1, 1,
  now(), 1426, 'stephenlin', '172.18.82.15',
  now(), 1426, 'stephenlin', '172.18.82.15');

  INDEX(user_group_id)

  INDEX(user_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ws_service_urls;
CREATE TABLE ws_service_urls (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  service_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  url                   TEXT NOT NULL,
  safe_search           ENUM('', 'Off', 'Medium', 'High') NOT NULL,
  descr                 TEXT NULL,
  qpm                   BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
  proposed_cpm          FLOAT(10,2) NULL,
  search_result_size    INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 10,
  languages             VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
  exclusivity           VARCHAR(128) NULL,
  branding              TEXT NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,

  department                   VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  cost_center                  VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  can_google_affiliates_order_under_contract
                               BOOL NULL DEFAULT 0,
  matter_tag                   VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  relationship                 ENUM('New', 'Existing'),

  -- Columns for Terms for Inbound: afc, cogs, corp, datacenter, event
  --                                marketing, other, insertion
  description                  TEXT NULL,
  robo_id                      VARCHAR(10) NULL,
  notes                        TEXT,
  is_click_to_accept           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  click_to_accept_agreement_request_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,

  -- Columns for NDA
  nda_changes                  ENUM('yes', 'no', 'na'),
  residuals_flag               BOOL NULL,
  residuals                    TEXT,
  governing_law                TEXT,
  venue                        VARCHAR(256) NULL,
  google_termination_for_convenience   BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  customer_termination_for_convenience BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  language_id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  effectivity_status           ENUM('ACTIVE', 'EXPIRED', 'PENDING', 'TERMINATED'),
  legacy                       BOOL DEFAULT 0,
  parent_id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  stipulate_parent_id          INT(20) UNSIGNED,
  product_area_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  governing_law_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  rivermine_contract_required  BOOL DEFAULT FALSE,
  is_sent_to_rivermine         BOOL DEFAULT FALSE;

  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  INDEX(agreement_type_id),
  INDEX(language_id),
  INDEX(parent_id),
  INDEX(partner_country_id),
  INDEX(requester_email),
  INDEX(requester_name),
  INDEX(state_province_id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(click_to_accept_agreement_request_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  pending_status_comments TEXT NULL,

#
# Create table to capture leads information
#
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS leads;
CREATE TABLE leads (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  partner_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  product_area_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  description        TEXT NOT NULL,
  requester_name     VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  requester_email    VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  department         VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  cost_center        VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  has_financial_commitment TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  created            DATETIME NULL,
  updated            DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  updated_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(id),
  INDEX(partner_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS lead_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE lead_audit_logs (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  lead_id             INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(lead_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tech_profiles;
CREATE TABLE tech_profiles (
  id                        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  target_completion_date    DATE NOT NULL,
  requester_id              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  requested_date            DATETIME NOT NULL,
  request_notes             TEXT NULL,
  accepted_date             DATETIME NULL,
  closed_date               DATETIME NULL,
  status                    ENUM('requested', 'accepted', 'closed') NOT NULL,
  updated                   DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip             VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                   DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip             VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS technical_approval_details;
CREATE TABLE technical_approval_details (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  trs_recommended             BOOL,
  trs_recommendation_result   ENUM('RE_WORK', 'NO_CHANGE'),
  comments                    TEXT NULL,
  updated                     DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                     DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS launches;
CREATE TABLE launches (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  launch_type        VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  deal_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  actual_launch_date DATE NOT NULL,
  summary            TEXT NOT NULL,
  google_maps_for_mobile              BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  google_maps_for_mobile_client_id    VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  gmail_mobile                        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  gmail_mobile_client_id              VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  gmapi_off_net                       BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  gmapi_off_net_client_id             VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  gmapi_on_net                        BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  gmapi_on_net_client_id              VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  gmapi_ads                           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  gmapi_ads_client_id                 VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  mobile_traffic_referral             BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  mobile_traffic_referral_client_id   VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  mobile_afc                          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  mobile_afc_client_id                VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  mobile_afs                          BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  mobile_afs_client_id                VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  mobile_yt                           BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  mobile_yt_client_id                 VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  youtube_api                         BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  youtube_api_client_id               VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  num_of_subscribers_or_users         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  num_of_device_model_launched        INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  num_of_device_model_launched_yt     INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  playback_statistics                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  traffic_volume                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  traffic_volume_unit                 VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  performance_statistics              TEXT NULL,
  performance_statistics_yt           TEXT NULL,
  updated            DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created            DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by         VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip      VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS launch_adsense_details;
CREATE TABLE launch_adsense_details (
  id                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  launch_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  client_id           VARCHAR(125) NOT NULL,
  service_type        VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  sites               TEXT NOT NULL,
  implementation      ENUM ('XML', 'JavaScript', 'IFrame') NOT NULL,
  implementation_note TEXT NOT NULL,
  from_date           DATE NULL,
  to_date             DATE NULL,
  queries             INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  coverage            FLOAT NULL,
  impressions         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  clicks              INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  ctr                 FLOAT NULL,
  rpm                 FLOAT NULL,
  updated             DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by          VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip       VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created             DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by          VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip       VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted             BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(launch_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS launch_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE launch_audit_logs (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  launch_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(launch_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS launch_adsense_detail_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE launch_adsense_detail_audit_logs (
  id                       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  launch_adsense_detail_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  primary key (id),
  INDEX(launch_adsense_detail_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS languages;
CREATE TABLE languages (
  id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name     VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL,
  code     VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL,
  deleted  BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  type                        VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  launch_id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  brand_code                  VARCHAR(125) NOT NULL,
  first_searches_per_day      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  installs_per_day            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  projected_downloads_per_day INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  distribution_channels       ENUM ('Web Offer', 'Bundle', 'OEM') NOT NULL,
  version                     VARCHAR(125) NOT NULL,
  platform                    ENUM ('Windows 2000/XP', 'Windows 98/ME') NOT NULL,

  updated                     DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                     DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by                  VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip               VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                     BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(launch_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- NOTE: See elsewhere in file for static data in the reference_terms table.

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS reference_terms;
CREATE TABLE reference_terms(
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  type               VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  name               VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  short_name         VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  parent_term_id     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  description        VARCHAR(256) NULL,
  sort_order         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 100,
  enabled            BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  is_system_term     BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(name),
  INDEX(parent_term_id),
  INDEX(short_name),
  UNIQUE INDEX(type, name, parent_term_id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(type, short_name, parent_term_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  paying_status_dnz            ENUM('UNINITIALIZED', 'PRE_SALES', 'PENDING',
                                    'PAYING', 'PLACEHOLDER', 'EXPIRED', 'TERMINATED',
                                    'DISAPPROVED', 'NA', 'UNKNOWN')
                                    NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UNINITIALIZED',
  paying_start_date_dnz        DATE NULL,

                                    'NEEDS_VALIDATION',

  assignable_entity     ENUM ('DEAL', 'PARTNER',
                              'DEAL_FOLDER', 'LEGAL_MATTER',
                              'MISC_MATTER', 'DEAL_MATTER', 'SPECIAL_APPROVAL') NULL,
  evaluate_mode         ENUM ('IN_ROLE', 'IN_ROLE_GROUP',
                              'IN_ROLE_ASSIGNED', 'IN_ROLE_GROUP_ASSIGNED',
                              'IN_ROLE_ASSIGNED_RESTRICTED', 'IN_ROLE_GROUP_ASSIGNED_RESTRICTED', 'ASSIGNED')
                              NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS delegate_conditions;
CREATE TABLE delegate_conditions (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  delegate_permission_id INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  security_operator     ENUM ('AND', 'OR') NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL auto_increment,
  condition_id          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  role_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  need_assign           BOOL NOT NULL default 0,
  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  UNIQUE INDEX(condition_id, role_id, need_assign),
  INDEX(id),
  INDEX(condition_id),
  INDEX(role_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
