-- ============================================================================
-- Views
-- ============================================================================
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS deal_bodies_using_client_ids_view;
CREATE VIEW deal_bodies_using_client_ids_view AS
SELECT
 db.id AS deal_body_id,
 db.name AS deal_body_name,
 p.id AS partner_id,
 p.name AS partner_name,
 GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT st.name ORDER BY st.name) AS service_types,
 db.effectivity_status_dnz AS deal_body_effectivity_status,
 db.effective_date_dnz AS deal_body_effective_date,
 db.termination_date_dnz AS deal_body_termination_date
FROM
 deal_bodies db
 JOIN partners p ON db.partner_id = p.id
 JOIN deals d ON db.id = d.deal_body_id
 JOIN services s ON d.id = s.deal_id
 JOIN service_types st ON s.service_type_id = st.id
WHERE
 st.uses_client_ids = 1
GROUP BY
 db.id;

# Provides raw data for most_recent_deal_body_deal_with_spm_view view.
# Must be done as a separate view since a view cannot contain a subquery
# in it.
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS deal_body_deal_with_spm_view;
CREATE VIEW deal_body_deal_with_spm_view AS
SELECT
 d.deal_body_id AS deal_body_id,
 MAX(d.effective_date_dnz) AS effective_date_dnz,
 MAX(d.id) AS deal_id
FROM
 deals d
 JOIN deal_team_members dspm
   ON d.deal_body_id = dspm.deal_body_id AND dspm.role_id = 9
WHERE
 d.effectivity_status_dnz NOT IN ('UNINITIALIZED','SCUTTLED','PRE_SALES')
GROUP BY
 d.deal_body_id;

# This view contains a mapping of deal body IDs to the most recent (by
# effective date) deal ID where the deal has an SPM on it and the deal
# is not scuttled or in pre-sales.
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS most_recent_deal_body_deal_with_spm_view;
CREATE VIEW most_recent_deal_body_deal_with_spm_view AS
SELECT
 d.deal_body_id AS deal_body_id,
 d.id AS deal_id
FROM
 deals d
 JOIN deal_body_deal_with_spm_view dbInfo
   ON d.deal_body_id = dbInfo.deal_body_id
WHERE
 ((dbInfo.effective_date_dnz IS NOT NULL
   AND dbInfo.effective_date_dnz = d.effective_date_dnz)
  OR
  (dbInfo.effective_date_dnz IS NULL
   AND dbInfo.deal_id = d.id))
GROUP BY
 d.deal_body_id;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS aurora_client_ids_view;
CREATE VIEW aurora_client_ids_view AS
SELECT
 ci.id AS client_id_id,
 ci.client_id,
 ci.approval_status,
 'PAYING' AS previous_month_paying_status,
 ci.paying_start_date_dnz AS paying_start_date,
 ci.paying_end_date_dnz AS paying_end_date,
 ci.created AS created,
 d.id AS deal_id,
 d.name AS deal_name,
 d.deal_type,
 db.effective_date_dnz AS deal_effective_date,
 p.id AS partner_id,
 p.name AS partner_name,
 db.id AS deal_body_id,
 db.name AS deal_body_name,
 db.effective_date_dnz AS deal_body_effective_date,
 db.termination_date_dnz AS deal_body_termination_date,
 GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT spm.username ORDER BY spm.username) AS spms,
 GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT spd.username ORDER BY spd.username) AS spds
FROM
 client_ids ci
 JOIN deal_bodies db ON ci.deal_body_id = db.id
 JOIN partners p ON db.partner_id = p.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_body_recent_deal_view recentDeal
   ON db.id = recentDeal.deal_body_id
 LEFT JOIN deals d ON d.id = recentDeal.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN deal_spds dspd ON d.id = dspd.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN users spd ON dspd.spd_id = spd.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_team_members dspm
   ON recentDeal.deal_body_id = dspm.deal_body_id AND dspm.role_id = 9
 LEFT JOIN users spm ON dspm.user_id = spm.id
GROUP BY
 ci.id;

#
# View for Aurora to conveniently see which users have SPM, SPD, FP&A, or
# Accountant access in Simba.
#
# SPD: role_id = 7
# SPM: role_id = 9
# FP&A: role_id = 60
# Accountant: role_id = 61
#
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS aurora_users_view;
CREATE VIEW aurora_users_view AS
SELECT
 u.username AS username,
 IF(SUM(IF(urg.role_id = 9 OR ugurg.role_id = 9, 1, 0)), 1, 0) is_spm,
 IF(SUM(IF(urg.role_id = 7 OR ugurg.role_id = 7, 1, 0)), 1, 0) is_spd,
 IF(SUM(IF(urg.role_id = 61 OR ugurg.role_id = 61, 1, 0)), 1, 0)
is_accountant,
 IF(SUM(IF(urg.role_id = 60 OR ugurg.role_id = 60, 1, 0)), 1, 0) is_fpa
FROM
 users u
 LEFT JOIN user_role_groups urg ON u.id = urg.user_id
 LEFT JOIN user_user_groups uug ON u.id = uug.user_id
 LEFT JOIN users ug ON uug.user_group_id = ug.id
 LEFT JOIN user_role_groups ugurg ON ug.id = ugurg.user_id
GROUP BY
 u.username;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS gnome_deals_view;
CREATE VIEW gnome_deals_view AS
SELECT
  deals.id AS "deal_id",
  deals.name AS "deal_name",
  deals.legal_name_of_contracting_entity AS "full_legal_name",
  groups.name AS "deal_group",
  GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT regions.name ORDER BY regions.name) AS "partner_region",
  GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT countries.name ORDER BY countries.name) AS "partner_country",
  GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT service_types.display_name ORDER BY service_types.display_name) AS "services",
  deals.notes AS "general_notes",
  GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT spd.username ORDER BY spd.username) AS "spd",
  ltm.username AS "ltm",
  legal_matters.basic_biz_terms AS "basic_business_terms",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(fec.id), "&dealId=", deals.id) AS "fully_executed_contract",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(ld.id), "&dealId=", deals.id) AS "legal_draft",
  deals.created AS "created"
FROM
  deals
  LEFT JOIN groups
    ON deals.group_id = groups.id
  LEFT JOIN deal_regions
    ON deals.id = deal_regions.deal_id
  LEFT JOIN regions
    ON deal_regions.region_id = regions.id
  LEFT JOIN deal_countries
    ON deals.id = deal_countries.deal_id
  LEFT JOIN countries
    ON deal_countries.country_id = countries.id
  LEFT JOIN services
    ON deals.id = services.deal_id
  LEFT JOIN service_types
    ON services.service_type = service_types.name
  LEFT JOIN deal_spds
    ON deals.id = deal_spds.deal_id
  LEFT JOIN users AS spd
    ON deal_spds.spd_id = spd.id
  LEFT JOIN legal_matters
    ON deals.deal_matter_id = legal_matters.id
  LEFT JOIN users AS ltm
    ON legal_matters.legal_team_member_id = ltm.id
  LEFT JOIN documents AS fec
    ON deals.id = fec.deal_id
   AND fec.document_type_id = 54
  LEFT JOIN documents AS ld
    ON deals.id = ld.deal_id
   AND ld.document_type_id = 116
GROUP BY deals.id;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS gnome_misc_matters_view;
CREATE VIEW gnome_misc_matters_view AS
SELECT
  mm.id AS "misc_matter_id",
  lm.partner_name AS "partner_supplier",
  lm.basic_biz_terms AS "basic_business_terms",
  agreementType.name AS "agreement_type",
  subType.name AS "agreement_sub_type",
  lg.name AS "legal_group",
  mm.requester_name AS "requester_name",
  mm.requester_email AS "requester_email",
  mm.department AS "department",
  ltm.username AS "ltm",
  mm.relationship AS "existing_contract",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(fec.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "fully_executed_contract",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(nda.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "nda",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(ld.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "legal_draft",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(internal_draft.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "internal_legal_draft",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(internal_final_upload.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "internal_legal_final_upload",
  CONCAT("https://simba.corp.google.com/download.do?cmd=download&docId=", MAX(internal_final_restrict_upload.id), "&miscMatterId=", mm.id) AS "internal_legal_final_restrict_upload",
  lm.completion_date AS "locked_date",
  lm.created AS "created"
FROM
  misc_matters mm
  JOIN legal_matters lm
    ON mm.id = lm.id
  JOIN legal_groups lg
    ON lm.legal_group_id = lg.id
  JOIN reference_terms subType
    ON mm.agreement_sub_type_id = subType.id
 JOIN reference_terms agreementType
    ON mm.agreement_type_id = agreementType.id
  LEFT JOIN users AS ltm
    ON lm.legal_team_member_id = ltm.id
  LEFT JOIN documents AS fec
    ON mm.id = fec.misc_matter_id
   AND fec.document_type_id = 54
  LEFT JOIN documents AS nda
    ON mm.id = nda.misc_matter_id
   AND nda.document_type_id = 5
  LEFT JOIN documents AS ld
    ON mm.id = ld.misc_matter_id
   AND ld.document_type_id = 116
  LEFT JOIN documents AS internal_draft
    ON mm.id = internal_draft.misc_matter_id
   AND internal_draft.document_type_id = 154
  LEFT JOIN documents AS internal_final_upload
    ON mm.id = internal_final_upload.misc_matter_id
   AND internal_final_upload.document_type_id = 155
  LEFT JOIN documents AS internal_final_restrict_upload
    ON mm.id = internal_final_restrict_upload.misc_matter_id
   AND internal_final_restrict_upload.document_type_id = 157
GROUP BY mm.id;

# View created for the launchcontrol application.
# It is a "raw" view because it does not perform a GROUP BY deals.id
# which would kill performance, so the GROUP BY is left to the caller
# to perform.
#
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS launchcontrol_deals_rawview;
CREATE VIEW launchcontrol_deals_rawview AS
SELECT
 p.id AS PartnerId,
 p.name AS PartnerName,
 d.id AS DealId,
 d.name AS DealName,
 d.pre_sales_status AS PreSalesStatus,
 db.id AS DealBodyId,
 db.name AS DealBodyName,
 g.name AS DealGroup,
 se.username AS SE,
 tam.username AS TAM,
 spm.username AS SPM,
 spd.username AS SPD,
 st.display_name AS Service,
 bizContact.email_address AS BusinessContact,
 techContact.email_address AS TechnicalContact,
 esdi.signature_status AS SignatureStatus,
 esdi.partner_signatory AS MocaSignatoryEmail,
 d.effectivity_status_dnz AS DealEffectivityStatus,
 db.effectivity_status_dnz AS DealBodyEffectivityStatus,
 ctry.name AS Country,
 reg.name AS Region
FROM
 deals d
 JOIN deal_bodies db ON d.deal_body_id = db.id
 JOIN partners p ON d.partner_id = p.id
 JOIN groups g ON d.group_id = g.id
 JOIN services s ON (d.id = s.deal_id AND s.deleted = 0)
 JOIN service_types st ON s.service_type = st.name
 JOIN legal_matters lm ON d.deal_matter_id = lm.id
 LEFT JOIN echo_sign_document_infos esdi ON lm.echo_sign_document_info_id = esdi.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_spds dspd ON d.id = dspd.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN users spd ON dspd.spd_id = spd.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_ses dse ON d.id = dse.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN users se ON dse.se_id = se.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_team_members dtam ON (d.deal_body_id = dtam.deal_body_id AND dtam.role_id = 3)
 LEFT JOIN users tam ON dtam.user_id = tam.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_team_members dspm ON d.deal_body_id = dspm.deal_body_id
   AND dspm.role_id = 9 /* SPM */
 LEFT JOIN users spm ON dspm.user_id = spm.id
 LEFT JOIN entity_partner_contacts bizDc ON (d.id = bizDc.entity_id AND bizDc.entity_type = 'DEAL')
 LEFT JOIN contacts bizContact ON bizDc.contact_id = bizContact.id
   AND bizContact.contact_type IN ('Business Contact', 'Business/Tech Contact')
 LEFT JOIN entity_partner_contacts techDc ON (d.id = techDc.entity_id  AND techDc.entity_type = 'DEAL')
 LEFT JOIN contacts techContact ON techDc.contact_id = techContact.id
   AND techContact.contact_type IN ('Tech Contact', 'Business/Tech Contact')
 LEFT JOIN deal_countries dctry ON d.id = dctry.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN countries ctry ON dctry.country_id = ctry.id
 LEFT JOIN deal_regions dreg ON d.id = dreg.deal_id
 LEFT JOIN regions reg ON dreg.region_id = reg.id;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS synthetic_areas_view;
CREATE VIEW synthetic_areas_view AS
SELECT
  d.id as DealId,
  d.name as DealName,
  d.is_standard_deal as IsStandardDeal,
  d.effectivity_status_dnz as Effectivity,
  d.date_moved_to_100_percent_pre_sales_status,
  d.actual_launch_date,
  d.expiration_date,
  d.effective_date_dnz,
  d.termination_date_dnz,
  d.created,
  d.updated,
  g.name as GroupName,
  st.name as ServiceName
FROM
  deals d
  JOIN groups g ON (d.group_id = g.id)
  JOIN services s ON (d.id = s.deal_id AND s.deleted = 0)
  JOIN service_types st ON (s.service_type = st.name)
  LEFT JOIN deal_regions dreg on d.id = dreg.deal_id
  LEFT JOIN regions reg ON dreg.region_id = reg.id
WHERE
  reg.deleted = 0;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS bi_transit_view;
CREATE VIEW bi_transit_view AS
SELECT
 d.id as DealId,
 d.name as DealName,
 d.created,
 d.date_moved_to_100_percent_pre_sales_status,
 d.deal_type,
 st.name as ServiceName,
 d.pre_sales_status
FROM
  deals d
  JOIN groups g ON (d.group_id = g.id)
  JOIN services s ON (d.id = s.deal_id AND s.deleted = 0)
  JOIN service_types st ON (s.service_type = st.name);


#
# Create a new contract templates table
#
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_templates;
CREATE TABLE contract_templates (
  id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name         VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,

  -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(name)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# Create a new contract template versions table
#
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_template_versions;
CREATE TABLE contract_template_versions (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  version_number        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  contract_template_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  summary               TEXT NULL,
  document_template     MEDIUMTEXT NULL,
  status                ENUM('PUBLISH', 'DRAFT') NOT NULL,
  var_json              TEXT NULL,
  term_length_json      TEXT NULL,
  signature_method      ENUM('ONE_PARTY_ESIGNATURE', 'TWO_PARTY_ESIGNATURE', 'OFFLINE_SIGNATURE'),
  language_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  governing_law_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  legal_entity_id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  order_form_required   TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,                                         
  fsa_approval_required BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  -- Audit fields
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  deleted                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(contract_template_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# Create a new template variable instances table
#
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS template_variable_instances;
CREATE TABLE template_variable_instances (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  name                  VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  value                 TEXT NULL,
  template_version_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  deal_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  approval_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  active                BOOL NOT NULL default 1,
  justification         TEXT NULL,

  -- Audit fields
  deleted                 BOOL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated                 DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created                 DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by              VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip           VARCHAR(16) NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(template_version_id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(approval_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# Create a new contract template version groups table
#
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_template_version_groups;
CREATE TABLE contract_template_version_groups (
    contract_template_version_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    group_id                        INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (contract_template_version_id, group_id),
    INDEX(contract_template_version_id),
    INDEX(group_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# Creating a new table for Simba API users mapping.
#
CREATE TABLE api_users (
  id                      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  external_username       VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  simba_username          VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
);

#
# Creating a new table for Simba DVIP workflow
#
CREATE TABLE dvip_deal_details (
  id                              INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  deal_id                         INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  dvip_deal_type                  ENUM ('ACF', 'UPFRONT') NOT NULL,
  upfront_service_type            ENUM ('DIRECT_ADVERTISER_UPFRONT', 'AGENCY_UPFRONT',
                                        'AGENCY_REPRESENTING_ADVERTISER_UPFRONT') NULL,
  level_deal_signed  ENUM ('PARENT', 'COMPANY', 'DIVISION') NULL,
  name                            VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  grm_id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  include_exclude_divisions       ENUM ('ALL', 'INCLUDE', 'EXCLUDE') NULL,
  division_info                   TEXT NULL,
  agency_name                     VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  agency_grm_id                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  upfront_geographic_scope        ENUM ('GLOBAL', 'REGION_ONLY', 'COUNTRY_ONLY',
                                        'REGION_AND_COUNTRY') NULL,
  region_list                     TEXT NULL,
  country_list                    TEXT NULL,
  acf_geographic_scope            ENUM ('LOCAL', 'GLOBAL') NULL,
  is_mobile_only                  BOOLEAN NULL,
  involve_standard_qual_spend_products  BOOLEAN NULL,
  custom_product_list             TEXT NULL,
  net_committed_qual_spend        BIGINT NULL,
  net_reserve_plan                BIGINT NULL,
  client_allowed_discount         DOUBLE NULL,
  discount_rates                  TEXT NULL,
  client_additional_discount      DOUBLE NULL,
  average_deal_incentive          DOUBLE NULL,
  client_bonus_imp                DOUBLE NULL,
  exception_amt_link              TEXT NULL,
  q1_min_spend                    DOUBLE NULL,
  q1_check_date                   DATETIME NULL,
  mid_point_min_spend             DOUBLE NULL,
  mid_point_check_date            DATETIME NULL,
  q3_min_spend                    DOUBLE NULL,
  q3_check_date                   DATETIME NULL,
  pct_employees_pass_GCP          DOUBLE NULL,
  is_YT_launched_in_country       BOOLEAN NULL,
  discount_ad_format_details      TEXT NULL,
  discount_tiers                  TEXT NULL,
--Delete current_disc_tier once the data is migrated post 3.0.6/3.0.7 release
  current_disc_tier               FLOAT NULL,
  fixed_rate_link                 TEXT NULL,
  has_upgrade                     BOOLEAN NULL,
  has_brand_channel_upgrade       BOOLEAN NULL,
  brand_channel_upgrade_allowed   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  has_masthead_channel_upgrade    BOOLEAN NULL,
  brand_masthead_upgrade_allowed  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  bart_advert_name                VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  json_tables_updated_time DATETIME NULL,
  program_year                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  leverage_ratio                  DOUBLE NULL,
  context                         VARCHAR(500) NULL,
  research_dollar                 DOUBLE NULL,
  research_count                  INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  research_type                   INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  workflow_approval_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  workflow_stage                  ENUM ('PRESUBMIT',
                                        'DEAL_EXPERT_REVIEW',
                                        'CROSS_FUNCTIONAL_REVIEW',
                                        'SPECIAL_APPROVALS_PRESUBMIT',
                                        'SPECIAL_APPROVALS',
                                        'APPROVED'
                                  ) NULL,

  # Audit columns
  updated                  DATETIME NOT NULL,
  updated_by_user_id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  updated_by               VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  updated_by_ip            VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,
  created                  DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_by_user_id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  created_by               VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
  created_by_ip            VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY(id),
  INDEX(deal_id),
  INDEX(dvip_deal_type)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_division_infos;
CREATE TABLE dvip_division_infos (
  id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id      INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  division_name VARCHAR(128),
  grm_id        INTEGER UNSIGNED,
  country_code  VARCHAR(20),
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_region_lists;
CREATE TABLE dvip_region_lists (
  id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  region    VARCHAR(20),
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_country_lists;
CREATE TABLE dvip_country_lists (
  id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  country    VARCHAR(20),
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_product_lists;
CREATE TABLE dvip_product_lists (
  id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id  INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  product  VARCHAR(128),
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_discount_infos;
CREATE TABLE dvip_discount_infos (
  id                 INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id            INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  discount_name       VARCHAR(128),
  discount_percentage FLOAT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS contract_template_owners;
CREATE TABLE contract_template_owners (
  contract_template_version_id           INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  owner_id                               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (contract_template_version_id, owner_id),
  INDEX(contract_template_version_id),
  INDEX(owner_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_country_discount_infos;
CREATE TABLE dvip_country_discount_infos (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id                     INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  country                     VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL,
  average_deal_incentive      FLOAT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  client_allowed_discount     FLOAT UNSIGNED,
  client_additional_discount  FLOAT UNSIGNED,
  client_bonus_imp            FLOAT UNSIGNED,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_workflow_approvals;
CREATE TABLE dvip_workflow_approvals (
  id                          INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_deal_detail_id         INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  stage                       ENUM ('DEAL_EXPERT_REVIEW', 'CROSS_FUNCTIONAL_REVIEW', 'SPECIAL_APPROVALS') NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_discount_tiers;
CREATE TABLE dvip_discount_tiers (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  dvip_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  starting_threshold    VARCHAR(20),
  discount_rate         DOUBLE UNSIGNED,
  PRIMARY KEY(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dvip_deal_detail_audit_logs;
CREATE TABLE dvip_deal_detail_audit_logs (
  id INTEGER(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  dvip_detail_id INTEGER(11) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  INDEX (dvip_detail_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS google_signatories;
CREATE TABLE google_signatories (
  id                    INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  user_id               INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  authority_scope       ENUM('MARKETING_CONTRACT') NOT NULL,
  signatory_type        ENUM('BOARD_LEVEL', 'COUNTRY_LEVEL', 'FUNCTIONAL_LEVEL', 'REGIONAL_LEVEL') NOT NULL,
  monetary_limit        LONG NULL,
  admin_first_name      VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  admin_last_name       VARCHAR(50) NULL,
  updated               DATETIME NULL,
  updated_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  updated_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  updated_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  created               DATETIME NULL,
  created_by_user_id    INTEGER UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_by            VARCHAR(32) NULL,
  created_by_ip         VARCHAR(16) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  FOREIGN KEY (user_Id) REFERENCES users(id),
  INDEX (user_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS legal_entity_google_signatories;
CREATE TABLE legal_entity_google_signatories (
  legal_entity_id       INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  google_signatory_id   INTEGER UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (legal_entity_id, google_signatory_id),
  INDEX (google_signatory_id, legal_entity_id)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
